[_line]
Type=0x01
;GRMN_TYPE: Roads/INTERSTATE, MAJOR_HWY/Primary, divided, limited-access highway, akin to an interstate in the US/Non NT, NT
UseOrientation=Y
LineWidth=3
BorderWidth=1
Xpm="0 0 2 0"
"1 c #4080FF"
"2 c #000000"
String1=0x05,Autostrada
ExtendedLabels=N
[end]
